Executive Yuan Stipulates Methods for Compiling Reports for Various Agencies; Compile a General Report to Announce to the Nation

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan believes that in recent years, all facilities of central and local administrative agencies have been based on seeking truth from facts in order to achieve rejuvenation. However, it is impossible to express the effectiveness due to the lack of detailed reports. It has now been decided that from this year onwards, at the end of each year, a general report will be compiled on the facilities and processes of the past year to announce to the nation. On the one hand, it will allow various agencies to consult and learn from each other for what should be promoted and what should be reformed, and it can also learn from the past to plan for the future. On the other hand, it will allow the people of the country to have a correct impression of the government's administrative situation. Recently, the specific methods have been stipulated, and the main points are as follows: (1) The reports of the various ministries, commissions, and local governments shall be sent to the Executive Yuan before January 31 of the final year. (2) When compiling the reports, emphasis should be placed on those that can increase the people's faith in the government, those that can express the government's spirit of active construction, and those that can enhance the international status. (3) The materials included in the report should be: A. the situation of local public security; B. the situation of people's livelihood, such as farmers' harvests, floods and droughts, trade situation, important construction; C. central work, and attention should be paid to those that have made significant contributions to the welfare of the people, those that can solve the special problems of the province and city, and those that have a trial or experimental nature. (4) The funds used for construction should be described in detail to show the government's efforts to develop the national economy. (5) Special attention should be paid to the promotion, demotion, merit, demerit, transfer, and relocation of personnel. (21st Central News Agency Telegram)

(November 20th)

The Countryside of Changshu (Part 2)

— Jin Yong

The Life of Farmers

The life of farmers in Changshu can be viewed in three aspects: In the southeastern villages, because it is all paddy fields, every farmer must go to the fields to learn many techniques such as water bail and rice transplanting. Men and women alike must possess this skill. Therefore, before a woman gets married, the man's family must ask if she knows how to "make a living," that is, whether she can go to the fields and work barefoot and with exposed legs like a man.

In the northwestern villages, because the land is slightly higher and there are fewer rivers and ports, the acreage planted is half rice and half cotton, and the work in the fields is more complicated. Generally speaking, men are in charge of the work in the paddy fields, and women are in charge of the work in the cotton fields. While the men are singing rice-planting songs, the women are hoeing in another cotton field.

In the sandbar area along the Yangtze River, the life of farmers is a different scene. Because more cotton fields are planted there, the farmers' strength is concentrated on planting cotton. That area often suffers from floods and typhoons, and the life of farmers is more difficult than in the two previous villages. However, when a good harvest comes, a joyful and encouraging atmosphere is rarely seen elsewhere.

Heaven and Hell

The gentry of Changshu stand in the clouds enjoying the blessings in their grand halls, while many farmers groan in pain in hell.

Changshu has an overpopulation, so the land cultivated per household is very small. According to the situation in the author's hometown—the northwestern villages—each household averages between five and ten mu. If a family has ten mu of self-cultivated land, it is considered a well-off family in the countryside; fifty mu is considered a small rich man in the village. A family of five, cultivating ten mu of land, averages two shi of white rice per mu, totaling ten shi, of which six to ten shi must be paid as rent rice. The remaining rice is for the consumption of a family of five, which is sometimes not enough. As for the money for seeds and fertilizer, it is impossible to cope without borrowing. A family of five, old and young, work hard for a year, and the result is only enough to make a living. If the year is good, they can recover some of the cost of seeds and fertilizer. If they encounter famine, they will have to go hungry. Under such circumstances, the farmers have already entered the hunger line, and it is even more extravagant to expect them to improve agricultural tools, plant superior varieties, and be clean and hygienic.

Generally, farmers cannot circulate financially and do not have money to buy seeds and fertilizers, so they often cannot cultivate and plant in time, which reduces the harvest. Some farmers can borrow dozens of dollars, but at least they have to pay interest monthly, plus various handling fees. Therefore, once a farmer is in debt, it is impossible to pay it off under high interest rates.

In recent years, famine, hunger, and poverty have made farmers lose their loyalty, honesty, and docility. They have nothing to pawn and nowhere to borrow. Therefore, they have taken actions of defaulting on rent and demanding rent reduction from landlords. Although the doors of the landlords' warehouses are open, there are very few people paying rent. The threats of rent collectors and the arrests of yamen runners are useless. A long string of farmers are detained in the detention center. Last year and the year before, several hundred tenant farmers were detained in the detention center. However, "oil cannot be squeezed out of stones," and the farmers' blood and sweat have dried up.

Page 5

Page 6

Current Commentary

The Mania of Military Expansion

— Hua

According to a Geneva dispatch from the National News Agency, based on the League of Nations' 1936 Armaments Yearbook, the expenses for military armaments of various countries in the world have recently become even greater than before. In 1935, the total amount of military expenses worldwide reached 5.4 billion yuan (US dollars). In 1934, it was only 4.9 billion yuan. In 1913, it was only 2.5 billion yuan. It can be seen that the recent mania of military expansion in various countries in the world has reached the highest peak in human history.

The ultimate result of such military expansion is undoubtedly a major international war. The cruelty of this decisive war, judging solely from the quantity of existing armaments in various countries, can be determined to exceed previous wars by countless times. But knowing that such a cruel disaster lies ahead, why do so many countries act like blind men on blind horses, rushing straight into that terrifying abyss? In war, the most suffering are the innocent people. Why don't the billions of people in various countries in the world think of some active rescue measures when such a great disaster is imminent? These two questions are even more worthy of concern for the people in our semi-colonial country, for the Chinese people who have many compatriots already being trampled and slaughtered by war-crazed aggressors.

The current mania of various countries expanding their armaments started in 1931. After the Manchurian Incident in 1931, the balance of power in the Pacific was completely shaken. On the one hand, the aggressor Japan spared no effort to loot all its resources to support its aggressive machinery. On the other hand, other countries along the Pacific coast also rapidly strengthened their own armaments for their own interests. In 1933, Hitler seized power in Germany. His military fascist policy, on the one hand, turned the entire German nation into a large barracks, and on the other hand, step by step, destroyed the Treaty of Versailles, which maintained the European international balance of power after the war. As a result, the whole of Europe was threatened by war, and all countries had to strengthen their own defenses for their own safety. In 1935, Italy, which also belonged to the fascist forces, launched the war of aggression against Abyssinia, regardless of all international treaty constraints. This war has continued until this year, spreading seeds of military conflict everywhere in Africa, the Mediterranean, and the Balkan Peninsula in Southern Europe. It has given a strong stimulus to the military expansion of various countries. Recently, the intervention of several fascist countries in the Spanish war, the cooperation of Germany and Italy in the Central European struggle, and the news of the conclusion of an alliance between Japan and Germany, two major military adventure countries in the East and West, all indicate that international tensions have reached an extraordinary level in the tide of military expansion. War is imminent.

However, in terms of the actual situation, except for a few military fascist countries such as Japan, Germany, and Italy, most countries do not hope for the outbreak of war. However, for the prevention of the imminent war, many countries only focus on strengthening their own armaments, forgetting to unite the forces of peace to resist the aggressors of war mania, which is obviously not enough. Therefore, the League of Nations has become an agency with only a name, and the collective security system has suffered successive blows. Now, the continuous expansion of military expenses in various countries has also increased the infinite suffering of the people in various countries. If this continues to develop into an unprecedented great war in the future, it will truly be the greatest tragedy in human history.

Obviously, the current tide of military expansion in the world is precisely indicating that various countries do not yet have a full understanding of the efforts to defend peace and prevent war. Only by working hard on the road of collective peace can mankind reduce the pain suffered from cruel wars.

The Locarno Question: Content of the Second British Note, Advocating Simultaneous Discussion of East and West European Issues, New Treaty Must Be Based on the League of Nations Covenant, German Ambassador to Britain Returns Home for Consultations

(London) According to responsible sources, the British government sent a note to the signatory countries of the Locarno Treaty, namely the governments of Germany, Italy, France, and Belgium, on November 19. The main content of the note is to clarify that the five-nation Locarno Conference is not sufficient without discussing the East European issue together with the West European issue, and firmly states that the East European issue should be resolved simultaneously with the West European issue. In addition, the note firmly states that the new Locarno Treaty must be linked to the League of Nations Covenant. Germany previously replied to the British note, advocating that only France and Belgium should conclude a non-aggression treaty, while Germany's security should be guaranteed by Britain and Italy. The current British note argues that the guaranteeing country and the guaranteed country should be completely mutual. The British note also suggests that the implementation of the security guarantee obligations contained in the new Locarno Treaty should be an exception in the event that the attacked country itself violates the Kellogg-Briand Pact. According to the previous German reply, objections were raised to the original provisions of the Locarno Treaty, which stated that an exception should be made in the event that the attacked country violated the League of Nations Covenant. However, although Germany has withdrawn from the League of Nations, it still recognizes the validity of the Kellogg-Briand Pact. Therefore, the current British note specifically suggests the above-mentioned exception method. In addition, the Italian reply advocates that the guaranteeing country and the guaranteed country should be mutual. In other words, if Italy assumes the responsibility of guaranteeing the security of other countries, it must also be guaranteed by other countries. The current British note will inquire again whether Italy's so-called mutual guarantee refers only to the guaranteeing country and the guaranteed country, or also includes the guaranteeing country and the guaranteeing country. This point needs to be further clarified by Italy. (Havas dispatch on the 21st)

(London) German Ambassador Ribbentrop recently returned to China by plane and is scheduled to return to his post within the next week. It is reported that Ribbentrop's trip is for the purpose of discussing the current situation in Spain and the two issues of the second resolution note submitted by the British government to the signatory countries of the Locarno Treaty on the 19th of this month, with the authorities of the country. (Havas dispatch on the 21st)

Pacific Aviation: Canada Will Also Handle It, Flight Distance Shortened by 4,000 Miles

Chicago: The president of the American Aviation Transport Association, Keller, stated in his speech to the National Trade Congress here today that a Canadian company is currently preparing to open a Pacific air route, which will go from Chicago to Shanghai via Winnipeg along a great circle route. German-Austrian Negotiations Concluded: Economic Alliance Will Be Revived, Germany Exchanges Military Supplies for Austrian Products, New Trade Agreement Will Be Discussed Again at the Beginning of Next Month

(Berlin) Austrian Foreign Minister Dr. Schuschnigg came here, the first official report of Austrian cabinet members to Germany in four years, and has completed his mission today. According to a press release, Dr. Schuschnigg met with German Foreign Minister Neurath several times to discuss the political, economic, and cultural aspects of the two countries. The two sides had harmonious opinions and decided to convene a meeting in Vienna on December 7 to conclude a new trade agreement in order to increase bilateral trade. The purpose of Dr. Schuschnigg's visit to Germany this time was to seek an economic compromise with Germany so that Austria's large-scale rearmament efforts could be realized. It is now agreed that Germany should purchase Austria's surplus milk and timber, both of which are urgently needed by Germany. Austria will purchase military aircraft, tanks, and heavy artillery from Germany. The former's negotiations were deadlocked because Germany wanted to purchase Austrian goods at low prices. (Reuters dispatch on the 20th)

(Berlin) Austrian Foreign Minister Schmidt's visit to Germany has been completed. Today, he and German Minister to Austria Papen took a plane back to Vienna. Foreign Minister Neurath and Chancellor Hitler's representative, Secretary-General of the Prime Minister's Office Messner, all went to the airport to see them off. Before his departure, Schmidt issued a statement saying, "The results of this visit to Berlin further prove that although there have been slight disputes between Germany and Austria in recent years, the unity of the two countries' races will never be broken because of this." Schmidt then expressed his gratitude for the warm hospitality of Chancellor Hitler, Aviation Minister Goering, and Foreign Minister Neurath, and said, "Thanks to Foreign Minister Neurath's friendly attitude and his rich diplomatic experience, we have been able to raise many outstanding issues between Germany and Austria, exchange opinions, and reach a common understanding on the principles and how to practically resolve them in the near future. What is even more important is that our meeting this time has found a way to strengthen the German-Austrian agreement and prepare for a more complete future. German Chancellor Hitler recognizes the great achievements of Austria's construction efforts, and Austria also expresses sympathy for Germany's actions to establish honor, freedom, and justice throughout the world. Sixteen years ago, I studied at the University of Berlin. I have witnessed the ups and downs of Germany from defeat to recovery." Finally, he said that the German-Austrian Agreement is actually a preparation for the progress of the entire Germanic nation. (Havas dispatch on the 21st)

Madrid Area: Rain and Snow Fill the Roads, War Stagnates, Both Armies Only Use Rifles and Machine Guns to Shoot, Rebels Promise to Expand the Neutral Zone

Madrid: It rained in Madrid today, and the visibility was poor. Rebel planes did not continue to bomb, and the military activities around the capital were not as intense as in the past few days. Residents took advantage of this temporary cessation of hostilities to busy themselves with clearing the debris blocking the streets so that firefighters and paramedics could carry out their work during the next plane bombing. Those with the danger of collapsing were pushed down, the bomb craters were filled, and the rubble was removed. Refugees carrying furniture fled to safe areas in an endless stream. The fighting near the Modelo Prison was intermittent, but both sides mostly used rifles and machine guns to attack each other. Occasionally, artillery fire was heard, and there were no significant changes in the positions in various places. There was heavy wind and snow in the Guadarrama Mountains and the Gredos Mountains north of Madrid. In some places, the snow was as deep as 20 inches, so the war had to be suspended temporarily (Reuters dispatch on the 20th)

Avila: A special dispatch from our reporter, the weather in the vicinity of Madrid suddenly turned cold today, and the rain did not melt. The National Army had to stop advancing and only used heavy artillery to bombard the central and southern districts of Madrid, taking the opportunity to consolidate its positions. The National Army authorities here hope that the weather will improve in the evening so that they can continue to take the offensive. As for the government army, although it has attempted to counterattack, it is only a local action and not a comprehensive battle plan. In short, there is no doubt that the current war situation is that the National Army is taking the initiative (Havas dispatch on the 20th)

Madrid: The restaurants here today posted notices saying "Goods Sold Out" due to the blockage of traffic between the capital and the provinces and the interruption of food sources. An Associated Press reporter witnessed many women and children crying and wailing in the streets and alleys because they could not bear the hunger. (National Telegraph on the 20th)

Germany Denies Signing a Secret Military Pact with Japan; Germany Values Friendship with China; War Against Russia Would Be a Losing Proposition; Joint Anti-Red Defense Is Another Matter

(Berlin) Regarding recent news from Shanghai that the German Ambassador to Japan solemnly declared Germany's emphasis on friendship with China, and stated that no agreement had been established between Germany and Japan, the Hutung News Agency reporter learned from authoritative sources here that Germany has not signed any agreement with Japan. As for the rumored military agreement between Germany and Japan, it is also inaccurate. (National Telegram, 20th)

Mr. Fu Housi, the Eastern Manager of the German Hutung News Agency, has repeatedly seen reports in recent days about the conclusion of a secret military alliance between Japan and Germany. Even the specific content has been rumored in various and inconsistent ways. In reality, this matter is completely groundless and malicious slander, and a malicious propaganda to smear the friendship between China and Germany. I hereby responsibly deny it based on the facts and detail the origins as follows:

There are those who do not want the increasingly cordial and solid friendship between the revitalized China and the newly emerging Germany under the leadership of Mr. Hitler to progress smoothly. They often spread rumors and fabricate untruthful reports to alienate the Chinese people from their enthusiastic European friend, Germany.

In the past two years, we have read such news dozens of times. Recently, newspapers have also reported that Germany has concluded a military alliance with Japan, that Germany and Japan have signed an anti-Soviet agreement, and that Germany is exchanging munitions for Manchurian soybeans.

I believe that such stupid and upside-down methods are an insult to the intelligence of the Chinese people. The spreaders of these irresponsible rumors have not taken into account the Chinese newspaper readers' own ability to judge, and hope to use this stereotypical and repeatedly appearing false news to gradually erode the Chinese people's trust in their honest friends. However, these people will hardly get their wish, because the Chinese people have a very accurate understanding and can judge what is true and what is false. Germany has always regarded such slanders with a smile. We know deeply that the friendship between China and Germany will not be damaged by this, because true friends are made after self-consideration. External rumors will never cause mutual suspicion and hesitation. Human experience and factual experience are known to everyone, and there is no need to repeat them.

My motivation for refuting this time is like a private friendship. If you are suspected by a friend, you must tell your friend, "Others are trying to destroy the friendship between us, but you know me and I know you can trust me." Regarding the news reported in the newspapers, I now ask, "Does Germany have a military alliance with Japan?" The answer and the indication of the matter can only be answered with "No."

Japan and Germany are separated by vast oceans, with the vast Soviet Russia in between. Furthermore, if a war between Germany and Japan against Soviet Russia were to really occur, then the German people would be dealing with the largest number of troops in the world, handling nearly nine-tenths of it, while Japan would only handle slightly less than one-tenth. Moreover, the entire value of Soviet Russia is not even comparable to the blood shed by a single German soldier. Let us also look at the map of Europe and we can see how difficult it was for Germany to break free from the shackles of the Treaty of Versailles recently. Furthermore, we can learn two facts from this: (1) To this day, there are still anti-German groups in Europe. If Germany engages in war with Soviet Russia, then this group will definitely rise up and attack its rear, causing Germany to be attacked from both sides; (2) The policy of our leader and Prime Minister Hitler is very clear: "Germany is willing to live peacefully with the world."

Unexpectedly, some people now claim that based on information from this side or that side, a military alliance between Germany and Japan is indeed a reality. I ask, what contribution can Germany and Japan make in a military alliance? If the Germans want to attack Soviet Russia, they must pass through the countries between Germany and the Soviet Union, which is not permitted by any of Germany's eastern neighbors. The distance between Germany and the Soviet Union is no less than the shipping route between Shanghai and Gansu Province.

There is also no reason for Germany and Japan to conclude a military alliance in the Pacific Ocean. We deeply know that this alliance will place Germany and Japan's global policies in opposition to those of Britain. Do we have other interests in the Pacific Ocean that would prevent us from exercising military policy in the Far East? I will discuss this in another article later. I repeat again: "Germany and Japan will never conclude a military alliance. There is no hope or possibility for this alliance to exist in German national policy or Japanese policy."

Now, some people say that Germany and Japan have signed an anti-Soviet agreement. I answer, "An anti-Soviet agreement is no different from a military alliance between Germany and Japan against Moscow." The reasons have already been stated above and will not be repeated. However, joint defense actions to prevent the Third International's attempt at world revolution are very different from the former. We say with a sacred and serious attitude that the inherent civilization of a nation will be destroyed by communism. The events of the Russian Revolution are vivid in our minds and can serve as a warning.

Thanks to the power of our leader Hitler, central Europe has been liberated from the red danger. Look at Spain today, where thousands of innocent hostages are being brutally murdered under the guidance of Soviet Russia. From this, we can understand what the future holds for countries under the Third International.

Let's talk about China. I once traveled all over Jiangxi Province. Everywhere I looked, there were corpses lying in the fields, and the villages were desolate and desolate. It was unbearable to see. Why is this? This is all done by the Communist Party under the "hammer and sickle" banner. The loss of China's population is more than a million. The number of farmers who live and work in peace, workers who support themselves, and scholars who have been brutally poisoned is countless. The Communist Party's firm policy is to incite internal warfare in several parts of China, hinder the construction projects of the central government, and make it difficult for it to devote all its efforts to protecting the honor of the country. However, Moscow's sweet words have ultimately failed, and the Communist Party is still China's mortal enemy. I now recall Xinjiang. Has Soviet Russia not already revealed its intention in that province, aiming to separate the entire province from the territory of the motherland?

Furthermore, in Europe, when Hitler first took power in Germany in 1933, the enemies of the new Germany suddenly discovered their valuable friendship with Soviet Russia. Germany did not care and still followed its path towards national freedom. But to this day, the European nations are glaring at each other, and they realize that Soviet Russia will cause them to perish. As Soviet Russia and the countries become increasingly estranged, Germany will inevitably gradually take a leading position for the countries that recognize the red danger in Europe and the world. Germany's defensive line against Soviet Russia is not limited to Europe. Germany's position is well known to the Chinese authorities. Even to Japan, Germany has explained its views on the red danger in detail and clarified that opposing communism is the common principle of the world revolution philosophy. But other than that, we have never considered anything else or established any facts. Japan has expressed satisfaction with our efforts to keep the red flames away from its borders. We must also solemnly declare here that Germany has no hostility towards the Russian people. We hope that this great nation will one day be able to break free from the shackles of communism and return to peaceful coexistence with other nations.

In addition, what is more dangerous is the slander created by our enemies that Germany is exchanging munitions for Manchurian soybeans. I answer to this: this is a dream talk and a fantasy.

Manchuria has been the only part of China that has produced soybeans for decades. We used to be the biggest customers of Chinese soybeans. Consider that Germany is an industrial country, with a population of 70 million in an area only as large as a large province in China. Germany has a large number of urban residents, and Germany cannot fully supply the fat they need. Therefore, it has established an industry specializing in the manufacture of fats, most of which are made from soybeans. The unfortunate disputes in North China not only affect China itself, but also cause Germany, which relies on Manchurian soybeans, to suffer. Without soybeans, we would still not be able to support ourselves. Furthermore, due to foreign exchange relations, we have to exchange power plant machinery, engines, medicines, etc. for soybeans. Chinese farmers in Manchuria also gain a layer of protection in their lives due to Germany's export of soybeans. There is no large-scale planting of soybeans in other parts of China, so we cannot buy them elsewhere.

To say that Germany supplies Manchuria with armaments or gunpowder is even more false and absurd. There is no such thing. This proves that Germany's actions are actually opposed to China. Japan has a huge armaments and gunpowder industry, so it would be more reasonable to say that Japan is doing it.

As a matter of fact, if Germany and Japan had a so-called alliance or agreement, then Germany would have recognized Manchuria. The facts are there, and Germany has never recognized "Manchukuo."

In terms of reasoning, Germany is developing a huge market in China, and it would never rashly take this rebellious action to cut off its future before it is fully achieved.

China's happiness can make Germany happy as well, because China's rising purchasing power can allow German workers to have jobs and wages, and Germany can also purchase its products from China. This is also what Chinese farmers and workers depend on for food and clothing. Germany's major industries need Chinese raw materials, and China's industries also need German machinery. Why would Germany want to destroy this friendship that concerns the lives of the Chinese people? Pacific peace is Germany's only policy here. We need peace to run our business, and we need business to survive. Since we need peace and business, we will never participate in any events that endanger our future and business. It goes without saying that China and Germany still have a long and difficult period of revitalization. I sincerely hope that the two nations can work together with all their strength, based on their past history and true friendship. (National Telegram, 21st)

Japan Establishes Manchuria Industrial Bank to Control Finance in the Puppet State; Capital of 30 Million Yuan; Tomita Appointed as President

(Nanjing) The Office of Manchurian Affairs announced that, in order to improve the financial institutions of "Manchukuo," the Japanese and Manchu governments have decided to establish the Manchuria Industrial Bank. After negotiations to purchase all the business of the Korean Bank (excluding those in the Kwantung Leased Territory) and the Manchuria Bank and Zhenglong Bank in Manchuria, all parties have understood the importance of national policy, and the cooperation has been successfully resolved. It can be realized within days. The Manchuria Industrial Bank is a special bank of "Manchukuo" with a capital of 30 million yuan in national currency, half of which will be paid in first (half by the "Manchukuo" government and half by the Korean Bank). In addition to general banking business, it also operates long-term financial business to smooth general finance. At the same time, for the purpose of developing various industries, its mission is to provide the necessary long-term, low-interest funds. And for the purpose of obtaining funds, it has the special right to issue bonds fifteen times its paid-up capital. If bonds are issued abroad, the "Manchukuo" government guarantees the payment of principal and interest to the Central Bank of Manchuria. Its mission is naturally different. We deeply expect the two banks to gradually adjust and cooperate with each other in their respective business fields, and each to fulfill their mission without regret. Although the Korean Bank has always shouldered an important task in Japan's policy toward Manchuria, this time, except for the Kwantung Leased Territory, all branches in Manchuria have been sold to the Industrial Bank. Therefore, in the future, it can be a sister bank, maintaining coordination and seeking common development. However, the convertible notes of the Korean Bank will naturally no longer be issued in "Manchukuo." This bank will be established roughly in early December, taking over the business of the Korean, Manchuria, and Zhenglong Banks, and is scheduled to open in early January next year. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Visits Taiyuan to Confer on Bandit Suppression Military Affairs in Suiyuan Province; Meets with Director Yan Twice; Spends One Night in Taiyuan and Returns to Luoyang

Taiyuan Dispatch: Chairman Chiang Kai-shek arrived in Taiyuan by plane from Luoyang on the afternoon of the 17th to meet with Yan Xishan, Director of the Taiyuan Pacification Headquarters, and the generals of Shanxi Province, to confer on plans for suppressing bandits in Suiyuan Province, and to inspect the recent situation of Shanxi's administration. He stayed in Taiyuan for one day, met with Yan twice, and returned to Luoyang on the 18th. The situation during his visit to Taiyuan is summarized below:

Welcome at the Airport

Deputy Chairman Yan, Madam Xu Lansen (Yan's wife), Chairman Zhao, and various military and government officials, including Supervisor Xu, Commander-in-Chief Yang, Chief of Staff Zhu, Secretary-General Jia, Commander of the 19th Army Wang Jingguo, Commander of the 33rd Army Sun Chu, Artillery Commander Zhou Dai, Garrison Commander Rong Honglu, Chief Advisor Kong Fanwei, Adjutant General Feng Pengzhu, Commander of the 13th Army Tang Enbo, Commander of the 34th Army Yang Xiaoou, Commander of the 7th Cavalry Division Men Zhizhong, Chief of Staff of the Four-Province Bandit Suppression Headquarters Mao Kan, and various section chiefs from Suiyuan, including Li Tao, Zeng Dunlian, Du Qiu, Director of the Provincial Education Department Ji Gongquan, Director of the Civil Affairs Department Qiu Yangjun, Director of the Finance Department Wang Ping, Director of the Construction Department Fan Xiangli, Provincial Committee members Li Shangren, Sun Huanlun, Wang Xiang, Secretary-General of the Provincial Government Wang Qian, Chief of the Police Department Xu Kuiyi, and Director of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau Cheng Shurong, etc., having received news of Chairman Chiang's arrival in Taiyuan, led all their staff to the airport in advance to welcome him. Various organizations, groups, and schools also lined up at the Xiaobeimen bus station to welcome him. Soldiers, police, and gendarmes were stationed along the route, with strict security measures in place. Merchants and residents throughout the city hung national flags to show their welcome.

Arrival in Taiyuan

At 2:40 PM, Chairman Chiang's plane flew in from the southeast, circling over Taiyuan once before landing at the airport outside Xiaobeimen at 2:50 PM. The planes carrying Chairman Chiang's entourage also landed shortly after. As the two planes landed, Chairman Chiang and his party disembarked amidst the sound of military music. Deputy Chairman Yan stepped forward to greet him, shaking hands and exchanging pleasantries in a very cordial manner. Chairman Chiang also nodded frequently to Chairman Zhao and the welcoming personnel. He then rode into the city with Deputy Chairman Yan in a car. At this time, the welcoming personnel also returned to the city by car. When Chairman Chiang reached Xiaobeimen, male and female students from various schools and civil servants from various organizations saluted him. Chiang raised his hand in response. After entering the city, he stayed at the Xingyuan on Xinmin Zhongzheng Street. At 3 PM, another part of Chairman Chiang's entourage arrived in Taiyuan by plane.

Entourage

Chairman Chiang, Deputy Chairman Yan, and Chairman Zhao chatted cordially in the Xingyuan for twenty minutes. Then, they summoned Supervisor Xu, Commander-in-Chief Yang, Chief of Staff Zhu, Commander Wang, Commander Tang, Commander Sun, Division Commander Men, and Chief Advisor Kong, a total of eight officials, and inquired in detail about the situation. At 3:10 PM, Deputy Chairman Yan, Chairman Zhao, and the other officials took their leave. Chairman Chiang personally escorted Deputy Chairman Yan to the courtyard. Chairman Chiang's entourage included Chief of the Adjutant Office Qian Dajun, Army Commander Wan Yaohuang, Senior Staff Officer Jiang Xiaoxian, Group Leader Zai Rizhang, Secretary Xiao Jinan, Adjutant Liu Jianyi, Guards Jiang Ruichang, Li Peiji, Staff Officers Liang Huasheng, Lu Zhongliang, Medical Officer Chen Fangzhi, as well as one telegraph operator, four special agents, five guards, and five servants, totaling more than twenty people.

Suiyuan Headquarters Banquet

At 7 PM, Deputy Chairman Yan hosted a banquet at the Zhonghezhai in the Suiyuan Headquarters to welcome Chairman Chiang and his party. Those invited included A Wang and Chairman Chiang's entourage, as well as Director Yan, Chairman Zhao, and other military and government officials below them. The atmosphere was very cheerful.

Chairman Chiang's Address

At 9:50 AM on the 18th, Deputy Chairman Yan went to Chairman Chiang's Xingyuan to pay his respects and discussed the military affairs of bandit suppression in eastern Suiyuan in detail, with full preparations already underway. At 10:30 AM, Chairman Chiang and Chairman Yan traveled together by car from the Xingyuan to the Suiyuan Headquarters. They summoned generals such as Chairman Zhao, Supervisor Xu, and Commander-in-Chief Yang in the Jingshitang to talk. At 11 AM, Chairman Chiang spoke in the Zisheng Hall of the Suiyuan Headquarters to the civil servants of the two Suiyuan offices, the New Life Movement Promotion Association, and various training classes. More than two thousand people listened to the address. Chairman Chiang walked to the Zisheng Hall, and the entire audience stood up to pay their respects. Deputy Chairman Yan presided over the meeting, leading the audience in performing the rituals and bowing three times to Chairman Chiang. Yan then delivered a welcoming speech, saying, "Today we welcome the Chairman with three meanings: first, to express our welcome; second, to express our admiration; third, to listen to instructions. We hope everyone will fully understand and faithfully follow the Chairman's instructions." Then, Chairman Chiang gave a detailed account of the international situation and the recent domestic situation. Finally, he encouraged all members to concentrate the strength of four hundred million people, bury themselves in hard work, strengthen themselves, unite, and complete their respective missions. The speech lasted for over an hour, and the language was extremely earnest and sincere. After the speech, he and Deputy Chairman Yan walked to the Zhonghezhai in the Suiyuan Headquarters to talk. At 12:40 PM, Chairman Chiang and Chairman Yan traveled together by car to the airport outside Xiaobeimen. Military and government officials, including Chairman Zhao, Supervisor Xu, Commander-in-Chief Yang, and A Wang, as well as representatives from various organizations, all went to the airport to see him off. At that moment, Chairman Chiang, amidst the sound of military music, exchanged a few words with the farewell party before boarding the plane and departing from Taiyuan. His entourage also boarded two planes and followed him. (November 18th)

Student Movement in Beiping Supports Suiyuan; Donates Salaries, Fasts, Raises Funds to Comfort the Troops; But Some Parties Express Dissatisfaction

Beiping Dispatch: It has been a week since the eastern part of Suiyuan was invaded by the pseudo-bandit army. Our soldiers are bravely defending the territory in the icy and snowy weather, with their positions as solid as mountains, which is truly admirable. Teachers and students from various schools in Beiping have successively donated salaries, fasted, raised funds, and sent telegrams to express their condolences and support. Details of the situation are recorded as follows:

At 4 PM on the 17th, the President of Peking University, Xu Songming, convened a discussion meeting of the administrative committee in the office. Xu Songming and deans Xu Shoutang, Zhang Yihui, Bai Pengfei, etc., attended. As a result of the discussion, considering the urgent situation in Guisui and the soldiers risking their lives, it was decided that all faculty and staff of the school would donate one day's salary, which is expected to amount to more than 2,500 yuan, to be remitted to the front lines for consolation. After seeking the consent of all faculty and staff, fundraising will continue. After the discussion meeting, the school sent a telegram to Chairman of Suiyuan, Fu Zuoyi, stating, "The invasion of Guisui is urgent, and Your Excellency's command is decisive. The whole country relies on you as a Great Wall. However, in this icy and snowy weather, the soldiers on the front lines are doing their best for the country. Our school colleagues have preemptively contributed one day's income to the front lines to express our condolences and support. The funds will be remitted separately. We send this telegram first." The students of the school also plan to organize a joint support association for Suiyuan soldiers from the five schools. After each school has organized separately, they will form a joint association. The Franco-Chinese University Support Association has been established and conducted large-scale street donations on the 18th.

From the 18th, students of Northeastern University reduced their breakfast portions and stopped heating for a week to save funds for the army. The students of the affiliated Beiping school of the university also launched a fundraising campaign and planned to unite with elementary schools in the city to organize a fundraising association for elementary school students to support Suiyuan. The Autonomous Association was established on the 17th and is responsible for handling everything.

In addition to saving on heating, teachers and students of Yenching University fasted for a day on the 17th. At noon, they swore an oath in the Great Auditorium to express their determination to support the Suiyuan soldiers. From the 18th, they suspended classes for three days and formed teams to walk into the city to expand fundraising.

The Fundraising Preparatory Committee for Aiding Suiyuan Soldiers, organized by teachers, students, and staff of major primary and secondary schools in Beiping, held a press conference at Linhuxuan in Yenching University at 3 PM on the 18th to report on the work plan. It is divided into four phases: the first phase is the 10,000-piece leather clothing movement, the second phase is the steel helmet movement, the third phase is the gas mask movement, and the fourth phase is the organization of a rescue team movement. It was also decided to expand fundraising, and the 19th to the 26th was designated as Fundraising Week. All members of the Fundraising Preparatory Committee and students of member schools will skip lunch to save money for aid and express their patriotic determination. At the same time, Yenching University, Beijing Normal University, and the Franco-Chinese University formed fundraising teams. Starting at 10 AM on the 18th, they went to various businesses and pedestrians in Beiping to solicit donations. There were about 200 people in 30 teams from Yenching University, including a women's team. There were 300 people in 30 teams from Northeastern University, with three, five, seven, or eight people in each team. The students who solicited donations all held small flags with white cloth and black characters and receipts. Their attitude was very amiable. Several hundred yuan have been raised on the 18th. A patriotic atmosphere has filled the ancient city. Mei Yibao, a professor at Yenching University, accompanied a student to Suiyuan by car on the evening of the 18th to inspect and comfort the soldiers.

Some parties were quite dissatisfied with the current aid-Suiyuan movement from various circles and have expressed informal opinions. The Beiping authorities believe that the actions of the students in this movement are all based on patriotic sincerity. However, on the 18th, some people claimed to be students from a certain school and solicited donations in the main streets of the city. After discussions, it was believed that the actions of the students had the following disadvantages: (1) It is impossible to distinguish whether those who are soliciting donations in the main streets are truly students. (2) Casual fundraising cannot be investigated. (3) Sudden stops of traffic in the main streets easily affect traffic order. (4) Inevitably, bad elements will infiltrate, distribute leaflets, and confuse the public. (5) Other incidents are most likely to occur. Based on the above reasons, this movement was stopped. The Beiping Municipal Government specifically invited the presidents of various universities, including Jiang Menglin, Xu Songming, Mei Yiqi, Lu Zhiwei, and Li Zheng, to a banquet at the Xihuatang of the Municipal Government at 6 PM on the evening of the 19th. However, due to Mayor Qin Dechun's presence in Bao to witness Feng Zhi'an's inauguration, he was unable to return to Beiping. Secretary-General Zhou Luan, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau Lei Sishang, and Director of the Public Security Bureau Chen Jiyan represented him. Song Zheyuan, fearing incidents in Beiping, also met with Han Fuqu in Nangong at 9 PM on the evening of the 18th before rushing back to Beiping to take charge of everything.

Amidst Anhui Province's Prohibition of Rice Exports, Large Numbers of Ships are Detained Mid-Journey; Rice Merchant Representatives Telegraph the Provincial Government to Thoroughly Investigate and Release Them

Wuhu Dispatch: Anhui Province had a bumper rice harvest this year, which is rare in recent years. Merchants from various places came to Wuhu to purchase rice continuously, and various industries also had a thriving outlook. However, although the amount of exports was far less than in previous years, rice prices, like other ports, rose rapidly, reaching more than nine yuan per stone, causing panic over people's food and high prices for all goods. However, after carefully examining the production and sales ratio, there is no doubt that there is a large surplus of rice. It goes without saying that this abnormal phenomenon is caused by someone manipulating hoarding for profit and other major reasons. After this autumn drought, the spring famine is approaching again. The Anhui Provincial Government, after repeated consideration, decided to issue an order prohibiting the export of rice from the province in case of emergencies. After this ban was announced, rice merchants from various parts of southern Anhui gathered in Wuhu and telegraphed various parties requesting the ban be lifted, as there was no concern that the province's food supply would be lacking. The provincial government also attached great importance to this matter and was carefully considering it. Unexpectedly, numerous rice ships carrying rice mid-journey were detained in Yuxikou, Xiliangshan, and Jinhekou in Hexian County due to the limited time for the implementation of the provincial order, which was difficult to fully communicate. Even wheat flour was obstructed mid-journey. The Wuhu flour company requested the Wuhu Chamber of Commerce to forward a request for release. Representatives of sailing rice merchants and rice milling shops throughout the province recently gathered in Wuhu for a meeting, stating that not only did Hexian County detain rice ships, but they also forcibly unloaded the rice onto land and detained hundreds of boatmen. The damage caused by this is immeasurable, and the public sentiment is extremely indignant. It was decided to telegraph the Anhui Provincial Government to send personnel to investigate and handle the matter, order the return of the original goods, and release the people and ships. The original telegram is as follows: "To Liu Jun, Chairman of the Anqing Provincial Government: In accordance with the provincial order prohibiting the export of rice, all counties should strictly comply with it. However, the provincial order has been implemented for only a few days, and the merchants' ships en route may not be fully informed. The handling should be differentiated. Recently, it was found that the Hexian County Government dispatched teams to gather ships anchored at various ports waiting for prices to Jinhekou in the county and forcibly coerced them. Those who complied would be allowed to pass, while those who opposed would be forcibly unloaded, mixing coarse and refined rice in one pile, and beans and wheat were not spared. There was no distinction between them, and they were splashed and scattered regardless. Over a hundred ships have been unloaded and over a hundred people have been detained. This kind of haste undoubtedly exceeds the original intention of the provincial order prohibiting exports. Moreover, all the merchant ships are still within the territory of the province. We do not know what the county government is thinking. Even if there is a slight suspicion of export, before the ban was issued, it would have been appropriate to order them to return. This would have been appropriate in terms of reason and emotion. In desperation, we earnestly request that you send personnel to investigate and handle the matter, and order the county government to be responsible for returning the goods and releasing the people and ships in order to reassure the business community. This would be in the public interest. Yuan Doushu, representative of the Anhui Provincial Sailing Office in Wuhu, Wu Wentang, representative of the rice industry, Gu Houfu, representative of the rice milling industry, and others bow. (November 19th)"

Land in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province Will Begin to Implement Land Value Tax; Can be Implemented After Land Registration is Completed; Field Tax Will be Abolished After Land Tax is Collected

Zhenjiang Dispatch: The Jiangsu Provincial Government believes that although land tax has been reformed repeatedly, it still follows the names of diagrams and silver rice, which are troublesome to calculate and unclear to the people. The procedures for handling are numerous, and malpractices occur from time to time. Although the provincial government has considered reform, it has been difficult to implement, so it has not been changed in the past twenty-five years. Last year, the Land Bureau was established to carry out land surveys, and this year, land registration began, which is being actively carried out. It is learned that the provincial government will implement land value tax after the completion of land registration, and the date of commencement will be the time when the collection of the previous field tax is abolished. The rules for collecting land value tax were previously drafted by the Jiangsu Provincial Finance Department and submitted to the provincial government for revision. There are thirteen articles, which will be distributed to various counties for compliance in the near future. The original text is as follows:

Article 1: All counties and cities that have legally carried out land registration shall organize land value tax in accordance with the provisions of Article 27 of the Outline of Land Administration Procedures for Various Provinces and Cities. Article 2: The organization of land value tax in various counties and cities in this province shall be handled in accordance with these rules in addition to the provisions of the Land Law and the Land Law Enforcement Law. Article 3: All counties and cities organizing land value tax shall immediately abolish the original field tax levied. Arrears of tax in previous years shall still be paid in accordance with the original regulations. Article 4: Land tax shall be paid by the land owner. If the land is rented by foreigners, it shall be paid by the lessee. If there is a pawn, mortgage, or fixed-term lease, it shall be handled in accordance with the deed or custom. Article 5: Land tax in various counties and cities shall be collected by the county and city departments. Article 6: The land value tax rate is specified as follows: 12/1000 for improved land in the city, 20/1000 for unimproved land in the city, 40/1000 for wasteland in the city, 8/1000 for improved land in the countryside, 15/1000 for unimproved land in the countryside, and 25/1000 for wasteland in the countryside. Article 7: Land value tax in various counties is collected in two installments. The opening dates for collection are specified as follows: (A) The first installment is May 1, and the second installment is September 1; (B) The first installment is June 1, and the second installment is October 1; (C) The first installment is July 1, and the second installment is November 1. The above three types of installments shall be selected by the county and city based on the actual situation. However, the date for the first collection of land value tax in each county and city may be proposed by the county and city separately and submitted to the province for approval. Article 8: Each county and city government shall distribute tax payment notices to taxpayers half a month or a month before the opening of each land value tax collection period. Article 9: The collection period for land value tax in each county and city shall be two full months from the date of collection. Those who fail to pay within the time limit shall be deemed as owing taxes, and cases may be summoned for recovery and handled in accordance with the provisions of Chapter 8 of Part 4 of the Land Law. Article 10: Land with outstanding taxes shall not be transferred in ownership or have other rights established. If the ownership is transferred or other rights are established without paying off the outstanding taxes, the current right holder shall be responsible for paying off the outstanding taxes. Article 11: The reduction and exemption of land tax shall be handled in accordance with the Regulations on Reduction and Exemption of Land Tax and the Regulations on Surveying and Reporting Disasters and Famines. Article 12: If there are any matters not covered in these rules, the provincial government may consult the ministry at any time and submit a request for amendment. Article 13: These rules shall be submitted to the central government for verification by the provincial government and submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval and implementation.

Suzhou Propaganda for Supporting the Suiyuan Movement

Various circles in Suzhou are very enthusiastic about the Suiyuan Movement. Suzhou Mingbao and other newspapers collect donations on behalf of others, and the amount is quite large. Public servants of various institutions are also in the process of saving money for fundraising. It was decided at that time that students from various schools would organize more than 200 propaganda teams, with five people in each team, to go to various places in the city to promote the movement to the public in order to awaken the public. Changzhou Provincial Department Inspects the Wuqing Road

The Wujin to Qingyang Highway has been completed earlier. Long-distance buses were originally scheduled to start operating on the 15th of this month, but the opening was postponed because the road surface engineering had not yet been inspected and accepted by the provincial department. On the 20th, Zhu Ming, an inspector sent by the provincial government, and Shen Baozhang, a secretary sent by the Construction Department, arrived in Changzhou from Zhenjiang, together with Shen Xue, the engineering director, and Li Jiayi, the chief of the second section of the county government. At about 1 PM, they took a small car to inspect and accept bridges, culverts, and road surface engineering along the way. By about 4 PM, the entire road had been inspected. The Wuqing Automobile Company believes that since the road surface engineering has been completed and accepted and all preparations have been completed, it has decided to open the Wujin to Henglin section on the 25th, with a one-way fare of 22 cents.

Wuxi Postal Bureau Private Soil Case Released on Bail

Gu Fuqi, a clerk in the parcel room of the local postal bureau, committed suicide at home by electrocution. His suicide note involved the issue of private soil, implicating ten people, including Tong Jiayao and Yang Dahui. After the conclusion of the interrogation by the Second District Security Command, it was determined that they were not related to the case and were allowed to be released on bail on the 19th of this month and regained their freedom. Shen Fengzheng, the director of the postal bureau, reported the situation to the Postal Administration, requesting instructions on reinstatement, as Tong and others were implicated for no reason. Tong and others also requested Director Shen to apply to the Administration for the allocation of their suspended salaries to maintain their livelihoods.

Price of Fine Yarn Rises

Recently, the market price of cotton yarn has become active again and has been rising daily. However, it is not as fierce as the surge last month. Affected by the Shanghai market, the local market price of cotton yarn has risen by one yuan. Actual sales are not very brisk. The sale of existing yarn from various factories is also not very active. Therefore, the market situation is not tense, and people's hearts are very firm. Also, the flour market situation is that raw materials are gradually becoming scarce, and prices are rising. Yesterday's opening price for Jiufeng and Shanlu brands was 3 yuan and 75 cents per bag. Most of the purchases are from Shaanxi and other places coming to Wuxi to purchase. The local sales are very slow.

Yangzhou County Districts Donate Salaries to Help Pay Military Expenses

Magistrate of Jiangdu County Ma Zhenbang, considering the serious situation in eastern Suiyuan, led all staff and police officers of the county government to donate one day's salary and remit it to the front lines for consolation. On the 20th, he ordered the district chiefs to comply and ordered them to submit the name list of all staff and police officers in their respective districts together with the donations to the county for forwarding.

Nantong Police Officer Commits Suicide by Shooting

Zhang Yuankai, a first-class police officer from the Public Security Bureau's Nanxin Market Police Station in Tongcheng, returned to the station after patrolling at 4 AM on the 20th and suddenly committed suicide by shooting himself to death. After examination by the court prosecutor, his body was claimed by his family for burial.

Thorough Investigation of Embezzled Stolen Money

The Fourth District Security Command believes that the amount of stolen money recovered in the case of the 15,000 yuan robbery of cotton in Xilan is short. The detective captain of the Nantong County Public Security Bureau, Yao Dangping, detective Yang Weiting, and patrol leader Zhao Yugui, were detained and sent to the court for thorough investigation. On the 20th, Prosecutor Liu interrogated them and confronted them with the bandit Ji Youfu, who was captured in the case. Yao and others were still held in the detention center.

Hangzhou Four Highways Completely Repaired

The Zhejiang Construction Department believes that the Tongjian, Jianjie, Jianlan, and Chunsui highways are important transportation routes between Zhejiang and Anhui provinces. Previously, due to the disturbance of bandits and the unrest in the local area, travelers were restricted. Now, as a result of the army's vigorous suppression, the bandit atmosphere has gradually been cleared. Old and broken vehicles have been recalled, and new-style passenger cars have been allocated to operate on these roads. All four routes can be reached directly without obstruction. Situations such as breakdowns in the middle have no longer occurred. Passengers in both provinces have praised the convenience, so the income from the transportation of goods has increased sharply.

Letter Received

Dear Editor, I recently read the Wuxi dispatch in the news section of your newspaper on November 18, with the title "Silk Factory Buys Children to Sacrifice to Chimneys." It stated that near Xintangqiao Township in Dongting Town, Second District, a local silk merchant, Bao, etc., raised funds to initiate the construction of a small silk factory with 120 silk machines. All the houses are about to be completed. However, Bao, etc., were misled by superstition and needed to hold a grand sacrifice to the chimney after the factory was completed. They had previously purchased a child from a certain family, raised him in the factory, provided him with meat every day, and prepared him to be sacrificed to the chimney. This inhumane act is deeply hoped to be stopped by the authorities, etc. Hearing this, I was shocked. This kind of groundless fabrication not only damages personal reputation but also makes people commit criminal offenses. In addition to submitting a request to the Wuxi County Government Public Security Bureau and the Wuxi Court to investigate according to law, I am afraid that false information will be spread. Therefore, I specially send a letter to request a correction. Sincerely, To the Chief Editor of Shenbao Newspaper, Qiju Silk Factory, Dongting, Wuxi.

Local News

Yesterday, Representatives from All Circles Convened a Meeting and Resolved to Form a "One-Day Movement Promotion Association," Recommending the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Government to Prepare as Standing Committee Members, and Designated Five Banks Including Central, China, and Jiaotong to Collect Donations

In order to promote the National Contribution One-Day Income Movement, the Municipal Party Department of this city specially convened representatives from various agencies and groups in the city at 2:00 PM yesterday (the 21st) in the department's conference room to discuss measures. Attendees included Tong Xingbai from the Municipal Party Department, Li Dachao from the Municipal Government, Lu Jingshi from the Garrison Headquarters, Pan Gongzhan from the Social Affairs Bureau, He Yuanming from the Certified Public Accountants Association (representing Jiang), Yu Zhenhui from the Municipal Farmers' Association, Huang Zaoxiong from the Municipal Education Association, Ye Xianggao from the General Labor Union, Yan Rensheng from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Jiang Jianbai from the China Cultural Construction Association, Zhang Xiamin from the Shanghai Branch of the Aviation Association, Weng Qingxiong from the Secondary School Advancement Association, Hu Fengxiang from the First Special District Citizens' Association, Gong Jingyan from the Second Special District Citizens' Association, Chu Yaohuan from the Local Association, Zhang Zanchen from the National Medical Association, Zhu Yanggao from the Physicians' Association, and Liao Maoru from the Middle School Advancement Association, among others. Tong Xingbai was publicly elected as chairman, and Gu Shaoyan as secretary. After the meeting began as scheduled, the chairman first reported on the meaning and necessity of promoting the one-day movement, followed by discussion.

(1) Passed the "Organizational Rules of this Association" proposal, resolved to amend and pass it. (2) Recommended standing committee members and principal and deputy directors of each department. (5) Recommended personnel to draft the promotion plan. (6) Recommended personnel to draft donation solicitation measures. (7) Recommended personnel to draft donation collection, delivery, and custody measures.
